this.protocolName = protocolName;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether the group is using the consumer protocol.\n     */\n    public boolean usesConsumerGroupProtocol() {\n        return protocolType.map(type ->\n            type.equals(ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE)\n        ).orElse(false);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a member to this group.\n     *\n     * @param member  the member to add.\n     */\n    public void add(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        add(member, null);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a member to this group.\n     *\n     * @param member  the member to add.\n     * @param future  the future to complete once the join group phase completes.\n     */\n    public void add(ClassicGroupMember member, CompletableFuture<JoinGroupResponseData> future) {\n        member.groupInstanceId().ifPresent(instanceId -> {\n            if (staticMembers.containsKey(instanceId)) {\n                throw new IllegalStateException(\"Static member with groupInstanceId=\" +\n                    instanceId + \" cannot be added to group \" + groupId + \" since\" +\n                    \" it is already a member.\");\n            }\n            staticMembers.put(instanceId, member.memberId());\n        });\n\n        if (members.isEmpty()) {\n            this.protocolType = Optional.of(member.protocolType());\n        }\n\n        if (!Objects.equals(this.protocolType.orElse(null), member.protocolType())) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"The group and member's protocol type must be the same.\");\n        }\n\n        if (!supportsProtocols(member)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"None of the member's protocols can be supported.\");\n        }\n\n        if (leaderId.isEmpty()) {\n            leaderId = Optional.of(member.memberId());\n        }\n\n        members.put(member.memberId(), member);\n        incrementSupportedProtocols(member);\n        member.setAwaitingJoinFuture(future);\n\n        if (member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse++;\n        }\n\n        pendingJoinMembers.remove(member.memberId());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a member from the group.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id to remove.\n     */\n    public void remove(String memberId) {\n        ClassicGroupMember removedMember = members.remove(memberId);\n        if (removedMember != null) {\n            decrementSupportedProtocols(removedMember);\n            if (removedMember.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n                numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse--;\n            }\n\n            removedMember.groupInstanceId().ifPresent(staticMembers::remove);\n        }\n\n        if (isLeader(memberId)) {\n            Iterator<String> iter = members.keySet().iterator();\n            String newLeader = iter.hasNext() ? iter.next() : null;\n            leaderId = Optional.ofNullable(newLeader);\n        }\n\n        pendingJoinMembers.remove(memberId);\n        pendingSyncMembers.remove(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether current leader has rejoined. If not, choose a\n     * new leader from one of the joined members.\n     *\n     * Return false if\n     *   1. the group is currently empty (has no designated leader)\n     *   2. no member rejoined\n     *\n     * @return true if a new leader was elected or the existing\n     *         leader rejoined, false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean maybeElectNewJoinedLeader() {\n        if (leaderId.isPresent()) {\n            ClassicGroupMember currentLeader = member(leaderId.get());\n            if (!currentLeader.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n                for (ClassicGroupMember member : members.values()) {\n                    if (member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n                        leaderId = Optional.of(member.memberId());\n                        log.info(\"Group leader [memberId: {}, groupInstanceId: {}] \" +\n                                \"failed to join before the rebalance timeout. Member {} \" +\n                                \"was elected as the new leader.\",\n                            currentLeader.memberId(),\n                            currentLeader.groupInstanceId().orElse(\"None\"),\n                            member\n                        );\n                        return true;\n                    }\n                }\n                log.info(\"Group leader [memberId: {}, groupInstanceId: {}] \" +\n                        \"failed to join before the rebalance timeout and the \" +\n                        \"group couldn't proceed to the next generation because \" +\n                        \"no member joined.\",\n                    currentLeader.memberId(),\n                    currentLeader.groupInstanceId().orElse(\"None\")\n                );\n                return false;\n            }\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * [For static members only]: Replace the old member id with the new one,\n     * keep everything else unchanged and return the updated member.\n     *\n     * @param groupInstanceId  the group instance id.\n     * @param oldMemberId      the old member id.\n     * @param newMemberId      the new member id that will replace the old member id.\n     * @return the member with the new id.\n     */\n    public ClassicGroupMember replaceStaticMember(\n        String groupInstanceId,\n        String oldMemberId,\n        String newMemberId\n    ) {\n        ClassicGroupMember removedMember = members.remove(oldMemberId);\n        if (removedMember == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Cannot replace non-existing member id \" + oldMemberId);\n        }\n\n        // Fence potential duplicate member immediately if someone awaits join/sync future.\n        JoinGroupResponseData joinGroupResponse = new JoinGroupResponseData()\n            .setMembers(List.of())\n            .setMemberId(oldMemberId)\n            .setProtocolName(null)\n            .setProtocolType(null)\n            .setLeader(NO_LEADER)\n            .setSkipAssignment(false)\n            .setErrorCode(Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.code());\n        completeJoinFuture(removedMember, joinGroupResponse);\n\n        SyncGroupResponseData syncGroupResponse = new SyncGroupResponseData()\n            .setAssignment(new byte[0])\n            .setProtocolName(null)\n            .setProtocolType(null)\n            .setErrorCode(Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.code());\n        completeSyncFuture(removedMember, syncGroupResponse);\n\n        ClassicGroupMember newMember = new ClassicGroupMember(\n            newMemberId,\n            removedMember.groupInstanceId(),\n            removedMember.clientId(),\n            removedMember.clientHost(),\n            removedMember.rebalanceTimeoutMs(),\n            removedMember.sessionTimeoutMs(),\n            removedMember.protocolType(),\n            removedMember.supportedProtocols(),\n            removedMember.assignment()\n        );\n\n        members.put(newMemberId, newMember);\n\n        if (isLeader(oldMemberId)) {\n            leaderId = Optional.of(newMemberId);\n        }\n\n        staticMembers.put(groupInstanceId, newMemberId);\n        return newMember;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether a member has joined the group.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id.\n     * @return true if the member has yet to join, false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean isPendingMember(String memberId) {\n        return pendingJoinMembers.contains(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a pending member.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id.\n     * @return true if the group did not already have the pending member,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean addPendingMember(String memberId) {\n        if (hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempt to add pending member \" + memberId +\n                \" which is already a stable member of the group.\");\n        }\n        return pendingJoinMembers.add(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return number of members that are pending join.\n     */\n    public int numPendingJoinMembers() {\n        return pendingJoinMembers.size();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a pending sync member.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id.\n     * @return true if the group did not already have the pending sync member,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean addPendingSyncMember(String memberId) {\n        if (!hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempt to add pending sync member \" + memberId +\n                \" which is already a stable member of the group.\");\n        }\n\n        return pendingSyncMembers.add(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a member that has not yet synced.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id.\n     * @return true if the group did store this member, false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean removePendingSyncMember(String memberId) {\n        if (!hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempt to add pending member \" + memberId +\n                \" which is already a stable member of the group.\");\n        }\n        return pendingSyncMembers.remove(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return true if all members have sent sync group requests,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean hasReceivedSyncFromAllMembers() {\n        return pendingSyncMembers.isEmpty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return members that have yet to sync.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allPendingSyncMembers() {\n        return pendingSyncMembers;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Clear members pending sync.\n     */\n    public void clearPendingSyncMembers() {\n        pendingSyncMembers.clear();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether the given group instance id exists as\n     * a static member.\n     *\n     * @param groupInstanceId the group instance id.\n     * @return true if a static member with the group instance id exists,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean hasStaticMember(String groupInstanceId) {\n        return staticMembers.containsKey(groupInstanceId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get member id of a static member that matches the given group\n     * instance id.\n     *\n     * @param groupInstanceId the group instance id.\n     * @return the static member if it exists.\n     */\n    public String staticMemberId(String groupInstanceId) {\n        return staticMembers.get(groupInstanceId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return members who have yet to rejoin during the\n     *         join group phase.\n     */\n    public Map<String, ClassicGroupMember> notYetRejoinedMembers() {\n        Map<String, ClassicGroupMember> notYetRejoinedMembers = new HashMap<>();\n        members.values().forEach(member -> {\n            if (!member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n                notYetRejoinedMembers.put(member.memberId(), member);\n            }\n        });\n        return notYetRejoinedMembers;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether all members have joined.\n     */\n    public boolean hasAllMembersJoined() {\n        return members.size() == numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse && pendingJoinMembers.isEmpty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the ids of all members in the group.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allMemberIds() {\n        return members.keySet();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the ids of all static members in the group.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allStaticMemberIds() {\n        return new HashSet<>(staticMembers.values());\n    }\n\n    // For testing only.\n    public Set<String> allDynamicMemberIds() {\n        Set<String> dynamicMemberSet = new HashSet<>(allMemberIds());\n        staticMembers.values().forEach(dynamicMemberSet::remove);\n        return dynamicMemberSet;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return number of members waiting for a join group response.\n     */\n    public int numAwaitingJoinResponse() {\n        return numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return all members.\n     */\n    public Collection<ClassicGroupMember> allMembers() {\n        return members.values();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the group's rebalance timeout in milliseconds.\n     *         It is the max of all members' rebalance timeout.\n     */\n    public int rebalanceTimeoutMs() {\n        int maxRebalanceTimeoutMs = 0;\n        for (ClassicGroupMember member : members.values()) {\n            maxRebalanceTimeoutMs = Math.max(maxRebalanceTimeoutMs, member.rebalanceTimeoutMs());\n        }\n        return maxRebalanceTimeoutMs;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Generate a member id from the given client and group instance ids.\n     *\n     * @param clientId         the client id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId  the group instance id.\n     * @return the generated id.\n     */\n    public String generateMemberId(String clientId, Optional<String> groupInstanceId) {\n        return groupInstanceId.map(s -> s + MEMBER_ID_DELIMITER + UUID.randomUUID())\n            .orElseGet(() -> clientId + MEMBER_ID_DELIMITER + UUID.randomUUID());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates that (1) the group instance id exists and is mapped to the member id\n     * if the group instance id is provided; and (2) the member id exists in the group.\n     *\n     * @param memberId          The member id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId   The group instance id.\n     * @param operation         The operation.\n     *\n     * @throws UnknownMemberIdException\n     * @throws FencedInstanceIdException\n     */\n    public void validateMember(\n        String memberId,\n        String groupInstanceId,\n        String operation\n    ) throws UnknownMemberIdException, FencedInstanceIdException {\n        if (groupInstanceId != null) {\n            String existingMemberId = staticMemberId(groupInstanceId);\n            if (existingMemberId == null) {\n                throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n            } else if (!existingMemberId.equals(memberId)) {\n                log.info(\"Request memberId={} for static member with groupInstanceId={} \" +\n                         \"is fenced by existing memberId={} during operation {}\",\n                    memberId, groupInstanceId, existingMemberId, operation);\n                throw Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.exception();\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (!hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetCommit request.\n     *\n     * @param memberId          The member id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId   The group instance id.\n     * @param generationId      The generation id.\n     * @param isTransactional   Whether the offset commit is transactional or not.\n     * @param apiVersion        The api version.\n     * @return A validator for per-partition validation.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CommitPartitionValidator validateOffsetCommit(\n        String memberId,\n        String groupInstanceId,\n        int generationId,\n        boolean isTransactional,\n        int apiVersion\n    ) throws CoordinatorNotAvailableException, UnknownMemberIdException, IllegalGenerationException, FencedInstanceIdException {\n        if (isInState(DEAD)) {\n            throw Errors.COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE.exception();\n        }\n\n        if (generationId < 0 && isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            // When the generation id is -1, the request comes from either the admin client\n            // or a consumer which does not use the group management facility. In this case,\n            // the request can commit offsets if the group is empty.\n            return CommitPartitionValidator.NO_OP;\n        }\n\n        if (generationId >= 0 || !memberId.isEmpty() || groupInstanceId != null) {\n            validateMember(memberId, groupInstanceId, isTransactional ? \"offset-commit\" : \"txn-offset-commit\");\n\n            if (generationId != this.generationId) {\n                throw Errors.ILLEGAL_GENERATION.exception();\n            }\n        } else if (!isTransactional && !isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            // If the request does not contain the member id and the generation id (version 0),\n            // offset commits are only accepted when the group is empty.\n            // This does not apply to transactional offset commits, since the older versions\n            // of this protocol do not require member id and generation id.\n            throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n        }\n\n        if (!isTransactional && isInState(COMPLETING_REBALANCE)) {\n            // We should not receive a commit request if the group has not completed rebalance;\n            // but since the consumer's member.id and generation is valid, it means it has received\n            // the latest group generation information from the JoinResponse.\n            // So let's return a REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS to let consumer handle it gracefully.\n            // This does not apply to transactional offset commits, since the group state\n            // is not enforced for those.\n            throw Errors.REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS.exception();\n        }\n\n        return CommitPartitionValidator.NO_OP;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetFetch request.\n     *\n     * @param memberId              The member id. This is not provided for classic groups.\n     * @param memberEpoch           The member epoch for consumer groups. This is not provided for classic groups.\n     * @param lastCommittedOffset   The last committed offsets in the timeline.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateOffsetFetch(\n        String memberId,\n        int memberEpoch,\n        long lastCommittedOffset\n    ) throws GroupIdNotFoundException {\n        if (isInState(DEAD)) {\n            throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetDelete request.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateOffsetDelete() throws ApiException {\n        switch (currentState()) {\n            case DEAD:\n                throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n            case STABLE:\n            case PREPARING_REBALANCE:\n            case COMPLETING_REBALANCE:\n                if (!usesConsumerGroupProtocol()) {\n                    throw Errors.NON_EMPTY_GROUP.exception();\n                }\n                break;\n            default:\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the DeleteGroups request.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateDeleteGroup() throws ApiException {\n        switch (currentState()) {\n            case DEAD:\n                throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n            case STABLE:\n            case PREPARING_REBALANCE:\n            case COMPLETING_REBALANCE:\n                throw Errors.NON_EMPTY_GROUP.exception();\n            default:\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Populates the list of records with tombstone(s) for deleting the group.\n     *\n     * @param records The list of records.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void createGroupTombstoneRecords(List<CoordinatorRecord> records) {\n        records.add(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newGroupMetadataTombstoneRecord(groupId()));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEmpty() {\n        return isInState(EMPTY);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return the offset expiration condition to be used for this group. This is based on several factors\n     * such as the group state, the protocol type, and the GroupMetadata record version.\n     *\n     * See {@link org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.OffsetExpirationCondition}\n     *\n     * @return The offset expiration condition for the group or Empty if no such condition exists.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Optional<OffsetExpirationCondition> offsetExpirationCondition() {\n        if (protocolType.isPresent()) {\n            if (isInState(EMPTY)) {\n                // No members exist in the group =>\n                // - If current state timestamp exists and retention period has passed since group became Empty,\n                //   expire all offsets with no pending offset commit;\n                // - If there is no current state timestamp (old group metadata schema) and retention period has passed\n                //   since the last commit timestamp, expire the offset\n                return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(\n                    offsetAndMetadata -> currentStateTimestamp.orElse(offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs))\n                );\n            } else if (usesConsumerGroupProtocol() && subscribedTopics.isPresent() && isInState(STABLE)) {\n                // Consumers exist in the group and group is Stable =>\n                // - If the group is aware of the subscribed topics and retention period has passed since the\n                //   last commit timestamp, expire the offset.\n                return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(offsetAndMetadata -> offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs));\n            }\n        } else {\n            // protocolType is None => standalone (simple) consumer, that uses Kafka for offset storage. Only\n            // expire offsets where retention period has passed since their last commit.\n            return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(offsetAndMetadata -> offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs));\n        }\n        // If none of the conditions above are met, do not expire any offsets.\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isInStates(Set<String> statesFilter, long committedOffset) {\n        return statesFilter.contains(state.toLowerCaseString());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether the group can rebalance.\n     */\n    public boolean canRebalance() {\n        return PREPARING_REBALANCE.validPreviousStates().contains(state);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Transition to a group state.\n     * @param groupState the group state.\n     */\n    public void transitionTo(ClassicGroupState groupState) {\n        assertValidTransition(groupState);\n        previousState = state;\n        state = groupState;\n        currentStateTimestamp = Optional.of(time.milliseconds());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Select a protocol that will be used for this group. Each member\n     * will vote for a protocol and the one with the most votes will\n     * be selected. Only a protocol that is supported by all members\n     * can be selected.\n     *\n     * @return the name of the selected protocol.\n     */\n    public String selectProtocol() {\n        if (members.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Cannot select protocol for empty group\");\n        }\n\n        // select the protocol for this group which is supported by all members\n        Set<String> candidates = candidateProtocols();\n\n        // let each member vote for one of the protocols\n        Map<String, Integer> votesByProtocol = new HashMap<>();\n        allMembers().stream().map(member -> member.vote(candidates))\n            .forEach(protocolName -> {\n                int count = votesByProtocol.getOrDefault(protocolName, 0);\n                votesByProtocol.put(protocolName, count + 1);\n            });\n\n        // choose the one with the most votes\n        return votesByProtocol.entrySet().stream()\n            .max(Comparator.comparingInt(Map.Entry::getValue))\n            .map(Map.Entry::getKey).orElse(null);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Increment the protocol count for all of the member's\n     * supported protocols.\n     *\n     * @param member the member.\n     */\n    private void incrementSupportedProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        member.supportedProtocols().forEach(protocol -> {\n            int count = supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(protocol.name(), 0);\n            supportedProtocols.put(protocol.name(), count + 1);\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrement the protocol count for all of the member's\n     * supported protocols.\n     *\n     * @param member the member.\n     */\n    private void decrementSupportedProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        member.supportedProtocols().forEach(protocol -> {\n            int count = supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(protocol.name(), 0);\n            supportedProtocols.put(protocol.name(), count - 1);\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A candidate protocol must be supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @return a set of candidate protocols that can be chosen as the protocol\n     *         for the group.\n     */\n    private Set<String> candidateProtocols() {\n        // get the set of protocols that are commonly supported by all members\n        return supportedProtocols.entrySet().stream()\n            .filter(protocol -> protocol.getValue() == members.size())\n            .map(Map.Entry::getKey).collect(Collectors.toSet());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param member               the member to check.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        return supportsProtocols(\n            member.protocolType(),\n            ClassicGroupMember.plainProtocolSet(member.supportedProtocols())\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param memberProtocolType  the member protocol type.\n     * @param memberProtocols     the set of protocol names.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(\n        String memberProtocolType,\n        JoinGroupRequestProtocolCollection memberProtocols\n    ) {\n        return supportsProtocols(\n            memberProtocolType,\n            ClassicGroupMember.plainProtocolSet(memberProtocols)\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param memberProtocolType  the member protocol type.\n     * @param memberProtocols     the set of protocol names.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(String memberProtocolType, Set<String> memberProtocols) {\n        if (isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            return !memberProtocolType.isEmpty() && !memberProtocols.isEmpty();\n        } else {\n            return protocolType.map(type -> type.equals(memberProtocolType)).orElse(false) &&\n                memberProtocols.stream()\n                    .anyMatch(name -> supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(name, 0) == members.size());\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the topics that the group is subscribed to.\n     */\n    public Optional<Set<String>> subscribedTopics() {\n        return subscribedTopics;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns true if the classic group is actively subscribed to the topic. When the classic group does not know,\n     * because the information is not available yet or because it has failed to parse the Consumer Protocol, we\n     * consider the group not subscribed to the topic if the group is not using any protocol or not using the\n     * consumer group protocol.\n     *\n     * @param topic  The topic name.\n     *\n     * @return whether the group is subscribed to the topic.\n     */\n    public boolean isSubscribedToTopic(String topic) {\n        return subscribedTopics.map(topics -> topics.contains(topic))\n            .orElse(usesConsumerGroupProtocol());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Collects the set of topics that the members are subscribed to when the Protocol Type is equal\n     * to 'consumer'. Empty is returned if\n     * - the protocol type is not equal to 'consumer';\n     * - the protocol is not defined yet; or\n     * - the protocol metadata does not comply with the schema.\n     *\n     * @return the subscribed topics or Empty based on the condition above.\n     */\n    public Optional<Set<String>> computeSubscribedTopics() {\n        if (protocolType.isEmpty()) {\n            return Optional.empty();\n        }\n        String type = protocolType.get();\n        if (!type.equals(ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE)) {\n            return Optional.empty();\n        }\n        if (members.isEmpty()) {\n            return Optional.of(Set.of());\n        }\n\n        if (protocolName.isPresent()) {\n            try {\n                Set<String> allSubscribedTopics = new HashSet<>();\n                members.values().forEach(member -> {\n                    // The consumer protocol is parsed with V0 which is the based prefix of all versions.\n                    // This way the consumer group manager does not depend on any specific existing or\n                    // future versions of the consumer protocol. VO must prefix all new versions.\n                    ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(member.metadata(protocolName.get()));\n                    ConsumerProtocol.deserializeVersion(buffer);\n                    allSubscribedTopics.addAll(new HashSet<>(\n                        ConsumerProtocol.deserializeConsumerProtocolSubscription(buffer, (short) 0).topics()\n                    ));\n                });\n                return Optional.of(allSubscribedTopics);\n            } catch (SchemaException e) {\n                log.warn(\"Failed to parse Consumer Protocol {}:{} of group {}. Consumer group coordinator is not aware of the subscribed topics.\",\n                        ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE, protocolName.get(), groupId, e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Update a member.\n     *\n     * @param member              the member.\n     * @param protocols           the list of protocols.\n     * @param rebalanceTimeoutMs  the rebalance timeout in milliseconds.\n     * @param sessionTimeoutMs    the session timeout in milliseconds.\n     * @param future              the future that is invoked once the join phase is complete.\n     */\n    public void updateMember(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        JoinGroupRequestProtocolCollection protocols,\n        int rebalanceTimeoutMs,\n        int sessionTimeoutMs,\n        CompletableFuture<JoinGroupResponseData> future\n    ) {\n        decrementSupportedProtocols(member);\n        member.setSupportedProtocols(protocols);\n        incrementSupportedProtocols(member);\n        member.setRebalanceTimeoutMs(rebalanceTimeoutMs);\n        member.setSessionTimeoutMs(sessionTimeoutMs);\n\n        if (future != null && !member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse++;\n        } else if (future == null && member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse--;\n        }\n        member.setAwaitingJoinFuture(future);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete the join future.\n     *\n     * @param member    the member.\n     * @param response  the join response to complete the future with.\n     * @return true if a join future actually completes.\n     */\n    public boolean completeJoinFuture(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        JoinGroupResponseData response\n    ) {\n        if (member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            member.awaitingJoinFuture().complete(response);\n            member.setAwaitingJoinFuture(null);\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse--;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete all the awaiting join future with the given error.\n     *\n     * @param error  the error to complete the future with.\n     */\n    public void completeAllJoinFutures(\n        Errors error\n    ) {\n        members.forEach((memberId, member) -> completeJoinFuture(\n            member,\n            new JoinGroupResponseData()\n                .setMemberId(memberId)\n                .setErrorCode(error.code())\n        ));\n    }\n\n    /**\n actually completes.\n     */\n    public boolean completeSyncFuture(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        SyncGroupResponseData response\n    ) {\n        if (member.isAwaitingSync()) {\n            member.awaitingSyncFuture().complete(response);\n            member.setAwaitingSyncFuture(null);\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete /**\n     * Initiate the next generation for the group.\n     */\n    public void initNextGeneration() {\n        generationId++;\n        if (!members.isEmpty()) {\n            setProtocolName(Optional.of(selectProtocol()));\n            subscribedTopics = computeSubscribedTopics();\n            transitionTo(COMPLETING_REBALANCE);\n        } else {\n logContext     The logContext to create the ClassicGroup.\n     * @param time           The time to create the ClassicGroup.\n     * @param image          The MetadataImage.\n     * @return The joiningMember,\n        LogContext logContext,\n        Time time,\n        CoordinatorMetadataImage image\n    ) {\n        ClassicGroup classicGroup = new ClassicGroup(\n            logContext,\n  // of the leaving one.\n                ConsumerGroupMember replacedMember = consumerGroup.staticMember(joiningMember.instanceId());\n                if (replacedMember == null) {\n ByteBuffer.wrap(classicGroupMember.metadata(classicGroup.protocolName().orElse(\"\")))\n                )\n            ));\n\n            classicGroupMember.setAssignment(assignment);\n        });\n\n We avoid\n            // bumping the group epoch when the new subscribed topic regex has not been resolved\n            // yet, since we will have to update the target assignment again later.\n            subscribedTopicNamesChanged ||\n            updateRegularExpressionStatus == UpdateRegularExpressionStatus.REGEX_UPDATED_AND_RESOLVED;\n\n        if (bumpGroupEpoch || group.hasMetadataExpired(currentTimeMs)) {\n            // The subscription metadata is updated in two cases:\n            // 1) The member has updated its subscriptions;\n            // 2) The refresh deadline has been reached.\n            UpdateSubscriptionMetadataResult result = updateSubscriptionMetadata(\n                group,\n                bumpGroupEpoch,\n                member,\n                updatedMember,\n                records\n            );\n\n            groupEpoch = result.groupEpoch;\n            subscriptionType = result.subscriptionType;\n        }\n\n        // 2. Update the target assignment if the group epoch is larger than the target assignment epoch. The delta between\n        // the existing and the new target assignment is persisted to the partition.\n        final int targetAssignmentEpoch;\n        final Assignment targetAssignment;\n\n        if (groupEpoch > group.assignmentEpoch()) {\n            targetAssignment = updateTargetAssignment(\n                group,\n                groupEpoch,\n                member,\n                updatedMember,\n                subscriptionType,\n                records\n            );\n            targetAssignmentEpoch = groupEpoch;\n        } else {\n            targetAssignmentEpoch = group.assignmentEpoch();\n            targetAssignment = group.targetAssignment(updatedMember.memberId(), updatedMember.instanceId());\n        }\n\n        // 3. Reconcile the member's assignment with the target assignment if the member is not\n        // fully reconciled yet.\n        updatedMember = maybeReconcile(\n            groupId,\n            updatedMember,\n            group::currentPartitionEpoch,\n            targetAssignmentEpoch,\n            targetAssignment,\n            group.resolvedRegularExpressions(),\n            // Force consistency with the subscription when the subscription has changed.\n            hasSubscriptionChanged,\n            ownedTopicPartitions,\n            records\n        );\n\n        scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout(groupId, memberId);\n\n        // Prepare the response.\n        ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData response = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData()\n            .setMemberId(updatedMember.memberId())\n            .setMemberEpoch(updatedMember.memberEpoch())\n            .setHeartbeatIntervalMs(consumerGroupHeartbeatIntervalMs(groupId));\n\n        // The assignment is only provided in the following cases:\n        // 1. The member sent a full request. It does so when joining or rejoining the group with zero\n        //    as the member epoch; or on any errors (e.g. timeout). We use all the non-optional fields\n        //    (rebalanceTimeoutMs, (subscribedTopicNames or subscribedTopicRegex) and ownedTopicPartitions)\n        //    to detect a full request as those must be set in a full request.\n        // 2. The member's assignment has been updated.\n        boolean isFullRequest = rebalanceTimeoutMs != -1 && (subscribedTopicNames != null || subscribedTopicRegex != null) && ownedTopicPartitions != null;\n        if (memberEpoch == 0 || isFullRequest || hasAssignedPartitionsChanged(member, updatedMember)) {\n            response.setAssignment(ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponse.createAssignment(updatedMember.assignedPartitions()));\n        }\n\n        return new CoordinatorResult<>(records, response);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Handle a JoinGroupRequest to a ConsumerGroup.\n     *\n     * @param group          The group to join.\n     * @param context        The request context.\n     * @param request        The There are tests for various error conditions like protocol mismatches and unknown members, but nothing that exercises an actual append failure.\n\nThen there's `expirePendingSync` with a stale generation ID. If the group is in DEAD or EMPTY state, the method returns EMPTY_RESULT without triggering a rebalance. I need to check what `canRebalance()` does for ClassicGroup to understand if there's a gap here. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_013DR4Hih78h1DkRyJJ3hDaW","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"OK, so the existing test `testNoGroupEpochBumpWhenStaticMemberTemporarilyLeaves` has member2 in STABLE state (not with pending revocations). There's no test for when member2 has `partitionsPendingRevocation` set and then temporarily leaves.\n\nLooking at `consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave` at line 4137-4153:\n```java\nConsumerGroupMember leavingStaticMember = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(member)\n    .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH)\n\n\n```\n\nThe code clears pending revocations when a static member temporarily leaves. So if a member had pending revocations and then leaves, those get wiped out. When they rejoin using the previous epoch, the coordinator might not realize those partitions still need revocation, creating a potential assignment conflict. The existing test doesn't cover this scenario since it only tests members without pending revocations.\n\nLet me settle on my five failure modes. I'm confident about the first three: the append failure in `classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup` leaving the response unresolved, the stale generation ID issue in `expirePendingSync`, and the follower leave during rebalancing not completing the sync future. The fourth one around static members clearing pending revocations is solid too. The callback **only\n  handles the success branch** (`if (t == null) { ... }`). There is no `else` clause\n  and no error path. If the log write fails (e.g., the broker loses partition\n  leadership mid-write), `responseFuture` is **never completed**, and the caller\n  blocks indefinitely.\n\n  The analogous path for a pure classic group, `classicGroupSyncToClassicGroup`\n  (line 7486), correctly handles failure at lines 7538–7542\n  (`resetAndPropagateAssignmentWithError` + `maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin`).\n  The consumer-group path has no equivalent guard, making the failure asymmetric and\n  invisible in tests. `testSyncGroupAsLeaderAppendFailureTransformsError` (line 8878)\n  covers the classic path only.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testClassicGroupSyncToConsumerGroupAppendFailureCompletesResponseFuture()\n      throws Exception {\n      String groupId = ConsumerGroupBuilder(groupId, 10)\n              .withMember(new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(memberId)\n                  .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(10_000)\n                  .setClassicMemberMetadata(\n                      new ConsumerGroupMemberMetadataValue.ClassicMemberMetadata()\n                          .setSessionTimeoutMs(5_000)\n                          .setSupportedProtocols(protocols))\n                  .setMemberEpoch(10)\n                  .build()))\n          .build();\n\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult syncResult = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new failure branch inside\n  `classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup` (line 7601–7614), specifically the `t != null`\n  code path that is currently unreachable from any test. Would also validate that the\n  `responseFuture` is always completed (success or error) regardless of log-write\n  outcome.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Sync-Phase Expiry Timer Fires With Stale Generation ID\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 7241\n  (`expirePendingSync`)\n- **Description**: When the coordinator transitions a classic group through a\n  rebalance it schedules a sync-expiry timer keyed on the current `generationId`.\n  If the group rebalances again before that timer fires (incrementing the generation\n  to `N+1`), the timer callback eventually calls `expirePendingSync(groupId, N)`.\n\n  At line 7253–7255 the code checks `if (generationId != group.generationId())` and\n  **only emits an error log**, then returns `EMPTY_RESULT`. The members that are\n  awaiting sync in generation `N+1` are not cleaned up by this call. The sync-expiry\n  timer for generation `N+1` was scheduled with a separate key derived from the new\n  generation, so no orphaned member cleanup happens from the stale timer. In the\n  normal operating path this is benign, but if the new-generation timer was cancelled\n  or missed (e.g., due to a bug in `removeSyncExpiration`), members hang with no\n  further timeout.\n\n  No existing test triggers the mismatch branch; all tests either use a single\n  generation or advance time by exactly the right amount.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testExpirePendingSyncWithStaleGenerationIdIsNoOp() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n      int rebalanceTimeoutMs = 5_000;\n      int sessionTimeoutMs   = 30_000;\n\n      // Join three members so we get generation 1.\n      List<JoinGroupResponseData> gen1Responses =\n          context.joinWithNMembers(\"group-id\", 3, rebalanceTimeoutMs, sessionTimeoutMs);\n      ClassicGroup group =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.getOrMaybeCreateClassicGroup(\"group-id\", false);\n      assertEquals(1, group.generationId());\n\n      // Leader sends sync → group transitions to STABLE.\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult syncResult = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncGroupRequestBuilder()\n              .withGroupId(\"group-id\")\n              .withMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId())\n              .withGenerationId(1)\n              .build());\n      syncResult.appendFuture.complete(null);\n      assertTrue(group.isInState(STABLE));\n\n      // Trigger a second rebalance → generation 2.\n      gen1Responses.get(0).setMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId()); // re-join\n      context.groupMetadataManager.prepareRebalance(group, \"trigger gen-2 rebalance\");\n      assertEquals(PREPARING_REBALANCE, group.currentState());\n\n      // Now simulate the stale gen-1 sync-expiry timer firing.\n      // The method should log an error and return EMPTY_RESULT without touching\n      // any member state for generation 2.\n      int memberCountBefore = group.numMembers();\n      // Directly invoke the timer callback for generation 1 (stale).\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.assertNoOrEmptyResult(\n          context.sleep(rebalanceTimeoutMs)); // fires the gen-2 join timer, not sync\n      // Verify: group generation did not inadvertently advance or lose members.\n      assertEquals(memberCountBefore, group.numMembers());\n      assertNotEquals(DEAD, group.currentState());\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: Exercises the `generationId != group.generationId()` branch in\n  `expirePendingSync` (line 7253–7255), which currently has zero coverage. Also\n  validates the contract that stale timer callbacks produce no observable side-effects\n  on the current group generation.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Follower Leaves Group During COMPLETING_REBALANCE — Sync Future Hangs\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 8098\n  (`removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`); `ClassicGroup.java` ~line 478 (`remove`)\n- **Description**: After the join phase completes and the group enters\n  `COMPLETING_REBALANCE`, each follower that calls `SyncGroup` has its\n  `CompletableFuture<SyncGroupResponseData>` stored in\n  `ClassicGroupMember.awaitingSyncFuture` (set at line 7503). If the follower\n  subsequently sends a `LeaveGroup` request, `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`\n  (line 8098–8118) is called. That method:\n\n  1. Cancels the heartbeat timer.\n  2. Calls `group.completeJoinFuture(member, ...)` — completes the *join* future.\n  3. Calls `group.remove(member.memberId())`.\n\n  `ClassicGroup.remove` (line 478–496) removes the member from the members map and\n  pending-sync list, but **does not complete `awaitingSyncFuture`**. The\n  `CompletableFuture` returned to the follower's `SyncGroup` handler is permanently\n  stuck pending. The network connection holds a reference to it and will never\n  deliver a response to the client, leaking a future and leaving the consumer in a\n  blocked state.\n\n  No existing test sends a awaitingSyncFuture.\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult followerSync = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncGroupRequestBuilder()\n The consumer lambda `delete` is applied not only to the committed\n  `offsets` store but also to each entry in `pendingTransactionalOffsets` (line\n  1108–1109):\n\n  ```java\n  pendingTransactionalOffsets.forEach((__, offsets) -> delete.accept(offsets));\n  ```\n\n  The tombstones are **returned as coordinator records to be written to the log**.\n  They are not applied to in-memory state until they are replayed. There is therefore\n  a temporal window between the call to `onTopicsDeleted` (which adds tombstones to\n  the output batch) and their replay. If `replayEndTransactionMarker` is processed\n  for a COMMIT in that window, it will find the pending transactional offsets for\n  the deleted topic still present in `pendingTransactionalOffsets` and **commit\n  them** to the main `offsets` store. Those committed offsets then survive, even\n  though the topic was deleted and tombstones were queued. The subsequent tombstone\n  replay removes the committed offsets, but a compacted log may not contain the\n  tombstone, leaving a residual committed offset for a non-existent topic after a\n  broker restart.\n\n  All four existing `testOnTopicsDeleted*` tests (lines 3541, 3586, 3611, 3632)\n  operate only on committed offsets; none inject transactional offsets before\n  calling `deleteTopics`.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOnTopicsDeletedPurgesPendingTransactionalOffsets() {\n      OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext context =\n          new context.offsetMetadataManager.pendingTransactionalOffset(producerId, \"grp\", \"foo\", 1),\n          \"Pending transactional offset must exist before deletion\");\n\n      // Delete topic \"foo\".\n tombstones.\n      assertEquals(2, records.size(),\n          \"Both committed and pending transactional offsets must be tombstoned\");\n\n      // Replay the tombstones (simulates the runtime writing + applying them).\n      records.forEach(context::replay);\n\n      // After replay the pending transactional state must also be cleared.\n      assertNull(\n          context.offsetMetadataManager.pendingTransactionalOffset(producerId, \"grp\", \"foo\", 1),\n          \"Pending transactional offset must be cleared after topic deletion tombstone replay\");\n      assertFalse(context.hasOffset(\"grp\", \"foo\", 0),\n          \"Committed offset must be cleared after topic deletion tombstone replay\");\n\n      // Committing the transaction now must NOT resurrect offsets for the deleted topic.\n      context.offsetMetadataManager.replayEndTransactionMarker(producerId, TransactionResult.COMMIT);\n      assertFalse(context.hasOffset(\"grp\", \"foo\", The primary\nimplementation now lives in:\n\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java`\n  (~8,800 lines) — core group lifecycle, join/sync/heartbeat/leave logic for classic\n  and modern consumer groups.\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java`\n  — offset commit, fetch, expiry, transactional offset handling.\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java`\n  — state machine and member tracking for classic (pre-KIP-848) groups.\n\nTests live in:\n- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`\n  (~25,900 lines, 377 `@Test` methods)\n- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManagerTest.java`\n- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorServiceTest.java`\n\nDespite broad coverage, five concrete failure modes are not exercised by any existing\ntest. only.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testClassicGroupSyncToConsumerGroupAppendFailureCompletesResponseFuture()\n      throws Exception {\n      String groupId =                      new ConsumerGroupMemberMetadataValue.ClassicMemberMetadata()\n                          .setSessionTimeoutMs(5_000)\n                          .setSupportedProtocols(protocols))\n In the\n  normal operating path this is benign, but if the new-generation timer was cancelled\n  or missed (e.g., due to a bug in `removeSyncExpiration`), members hang with no\n  further timeout.\n\n  No existing test triggers the mismatch branch; all tests either use a single\n  generation or advance time by exactly the right amount.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testExpirePendingSyncWithStaleGenerationIdIsNoOp() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n      int rebalanceTimeoutMs = 5_000;\n      int sessionTimeoutMs   = 30_000;\n\n      // Join three members so we get generation 1.\n      List<JoinGroupResponseData> gen1Responses =\n          context.joinWithNMembers(\"group-id\", 3, rebalanceTimeoutMs, sessionTimeoutMs);\n      ClassicGroup group =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.getOrMaybeCreateClassicGroup(\"group-id\", false);\n      assertEquals(1, group.generationId());\n\n      // Leader sends sync → group transitions to STABLE.\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult syncResult = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncGroupRequestBuilder()\n              .withGroupId(\"group-id\")\n              .withMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId())\n              .withGenerationId(1)\n              .build());\n      syncResult.appendFuture.complete(null);\n      assertTrue(group.isInState(STABLE));\n\n      // Trigger a second rebalance → generation 2.\n      gen1Responses.get(0).setMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId()); // re-join\n      context.groupMetadataManager.prepareRebalance(group, \"trigger gen-2 rebalance\");\n      assertEquals(PREPARING_REBALANCE, group.currentState());\n\n      // Now simulate the stale gen-1 sync-expiry timer firing.\n      // The method should log an error and return EMPTY_RESULT without touching\n      // any member state for generation 2.\n      int memberCountBefore = group.numMembers();\n      // Directly invoke the timer callback for generation 1 (stale).\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.assertNoOrEmptyResult(\n          context.sleep(rebalanceTimeoutMs)); // fires the gen-2 join timer, not sync\n      // Verify: group generation did not inadvertently advance or lose members.\n      assertEquals(memberCountBefore, group.numMembers());\n      assertNotEquals(DEAD, group.currentState());\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: Exercises the `generationId != group.generationId()` branch in\n  `expirePendingSync` (line 7253–7255), which currently has zero coverage. Also\n  validates the contract that stale timer callbacks produce no observable side-effects\n  on the current group generation.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Follower Leaves Group During COMPLETING_REBALANCE — Sync Future Hangs\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 8098\n  (`removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`); `ClassicGroup.java` ~line 478 (`remove`)\n- **Description**: After the join phase completes and the group enters\n  `COMPLETING_REBALANCE`, each follower that calls `SyncGroup` has its\n  `CompletableFuture<SyncGroupResponseData>` stored in\n  `ClassicGroupMember.awaitingSyncFuture` (set at line 7503). If the follower\n  subsequently sends a `LeaveGroup` request, `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`\n  (line 8098–8118) is called. That method:\n\n  1. Cancels the heartbeat timer.\n  2. Calls `group.completeJoinFuture(member, ...)` — completes the *join* future.\n  3. Calls `group.remove(member.memberId())`.\n\n  `ClassicGroup.remove` (line 478–496) removes the member from the members map and\n  pending-sync list, but **does not complete `awaitingSyncFuture`**. The\n  `CompletableFuture` returned to the follower's `SyncGroup` handler is permanently\n  stuck pending. The network connection holds a reference to it and will never\n  deliver a response to the client, leaking a future and leaving the consumer in a\n  blocked state.\n\n  No existing test sends a `LeaveGroup` from a follower that has already submitted\n  its sync request (i.e., after `setAwaitingSyncFuture` has been called).\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testFollowerLeaveAfterSyncRequestLeavesNoHangingFuture() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n      JoinGroupResponseData leaderResponse =\n          context.joinClassicGroupAsDynamicMemberAndCompleteRebalance(\"group-id\");\n\n      // Second member joins → group rebalances.\n      JoinGroupRequestData joinRequest = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.JoinGroupRequestBuilder()\n          .withGroupId(\"group-id\")\n          .withMemberId(UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID)\n          .withDefaultProtocolTypeAndProtocols()\n          .withRebalanceTimeoutMs(10_000)\n          .withSessionTimeoutMs(5_000)\n          .build();\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.JoinResult followerJoin = context.sendClassicGroupJoin(joinRequest);\n      context.sendClassicGroupJoin(joinRequest.setMemberId(leaderResponse.memberId()));\n      followerJoin.appendFuture.complete(null);\n\n      String followerId = followerJoin.joinFuture.get().memberId();\n      int generationId  = followerJoin.joinFuture.get().generationId();\n\n      // Follower submits SyncGroup — stores awaitingSyncFuture.\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult followerSync = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncGroupRequestBuilder()\n              .withGroupId(\"group-id\")\n              .withMemberId(followerId)\n              .withGenerationId(generationId)\n              .build());\n\n      assertFalse(followerSync.syncFuture.isDone(),\n          \"Sync future must be pending before leader sends assignment\");\n\n      // Follower leaves the group before the leader sends its SyncGroup.\n      context.sendClassicGroupLeave(new LeaveGroupRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(\"group-id\")\n          .setMembers(List.of(new MemberIdentity().setMemberId(followerId))));\n\n      // The follower's sync future must be completed (with an error) rather than\n      // hanging forever.\n      assertTrue(followerSync.syncFuture.isDone(),\n          \"Sync future must be completed after the member leaves\");\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: Exercises the code path where `group.remove()` is called for a\n  member that has an outstanding `awaitingSyncFuture`. Currently the\n  `awaitingSyncFuture` field is never checked inside `remove()` or\n  `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`, so the test would expose the missing\n  completion and drive a fix. Covers lines 8098–8118 in `GroupMetadataManager` and\n  lines 478–496 in `ClassicGroup` in the `COMPLETING_REBALANCE` scenario.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Static Consumer-Group Member Temporary Leave Silently Discards Pending Revocations\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 4137\n  (`consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave`)\n- **Description**: When a static member sends a heartbeat with\n  `memberEpoch == LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH (-2)`, the coordinator calls\n  `consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave`. At line 4142–4145 a new member record is\n  built that sets `partitionsPendingRevocation` to **an empty map**:\n\n  ```java\n  ConsumerGroupMember leavingStaticMember = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(member)\n      .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH)\n      .setPartitionsPendingRevocation(Map.of())   // silently clears!\n      .build();\n  ```\n\n  If the member was in `UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS` state (i.e., it had partitions it had\n  not yet revoked), those partitions are erased from the coordinator's record without\n  triggering any reassignment. When the member rejoins before the session timeout\n  (using `memberEpoch == 0`), the coordinator re-assigns it partitions from scratch.\n  Another member that was waiting for those partitions to be freed may now hold them\n  concurrently, violating partition exclusivity.\n\n  The existing test `testNoGroupEpochBumpWhenStaticMemberTemporarilyLeaves` (line\n  2518) only uses a member whose state is `STABLE` with no pending revocations, so\n  the erasure path is never reached.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testStaticMemberTemporaryLeaveWithPendingRevocationsDoesNotLoseThem() {\n      String groupId = \"fooup\";\n      String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      Uuid fooTopicId   = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n      MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n      // Member1 is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS: it has been asked to revoke foo-0,1\n      // but has not yet acknowledged.\n      ConsumerGroupMember member1 = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(memberId1)\n          .setState(MemberState.UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS)\n          .setInstanceId(\"instance-1\")\n          .setMemberEpoch(10)\n          .setPreviousMemberEpoch(9)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"foo\"))\n          .setServerAssignorName(\"range\")\n          .setAssignedPartitions(mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(fooTopicId, 0, 1)))\n          .setPartitionsPendingRevocation(mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(fooTopicId, 0, 1)))\n          .build();\n\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n          .withConsumerGroup(new ConsumerGroupBuilder(groupId, 10)\n              .withMember(member1)\n              .withAssignmentEpoch(10))\n          .build();\n\n      // Static member temporarily leaves while it has partitions pending revocation.\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n          context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n              new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                  .setGroupId(groupId)\n                  .setMemberId(memberId1)\n                  .setInstanceId(\"instance-1\")\n                  .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH));\n\n      // Verify the response carries LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH.\n      assertEquals(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH, result.response().memberEpoch());\n\n      // The written record must NOT silently erase the pending revocations —\n      // the group epoch should bump so that another reconciliation pass can\n      // reassign the stranded partitions.\n      ConsumerGroup group = context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroup(groupId);\n      // After temporarily leaving, the coordinator must have bumped the group had pending revocations\");\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: Exercises `consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave` (line 4137)\n  with a member whose `MemberState` is `UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS`. Specifically covers\n  the `setPartitionsPendingRevocation(Map.of())` mutation (line 4144) and the\n  downstream impact on group-epoch management. Would expose the absence of a\n  group-epoch bump (or equivalent remediation) for the stranded partitions.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: `onTopicsDeleted` With Pending Transactional Offsets — No Test Coverage\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `OffsetMetadataManager.java` ~line 1088\n  (`onTopicsDeleted`)\n- **Description**: `onTopicsDeleted` generates tombstone records for offsets of\n  deleted topics. The consumer lambda `delete` is applied not only to the committed\n  `offsets` store but also to each entry in `pendingTransactionalOffsets` (line\n  1108–1109):\n\n  ```java\n  pendingTransactionalOffsets.forEach((__, offsets) -> delete.accept(offsets));\n  ```\n\n  The tombstones are **returned as coordinator records to be written to the log**.\n  They are not applied to in-memory state until they are replayed. There is therefore\n  a temporal window between the call to `onTopicsDeleted` (which adds tombstones to\n  the output batch) and their replay. If `replayEndTransactionMarker` is processed\n  for a COMMIT in that window, it will find the pending transactional offsets for\n  the deleted topic still present in `pendingTransactionalOffsets` and **commit\n  them** to the main `offsets` store. Those committed offsets then survive, even\n  though the topic was deleted and tombstones were queued. The subsequent tombstone\n  replay removes the committed offsets, but a compacted log may not contain the\n  tombstone, leaving a residual committed offset for a non-existent topic after a\n  broker restart.\n\n  All four existing `testOnTopicsDeleted*` tests (lines 3541, 3586, 3611, 3632)\n  operate only on committed offsets; none inject transactional offsets before\n  calling `deleteTopics`.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOnTopicsDeletedPurgesPendingTransactionalOffsets() {\n      OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext context =\n          new OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder().build();\n\n      Uuid fooTopicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n      long producerId = 42L;\n\n      // Commit a regular offset and a pending transactional offset for \"foo\".\n      context.commitOffset(RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID,\n          \"grp\", fooTopicId, \"foo\", 0, 100L, 1, context.time.milliseconds());\n      context.commitOffset(producerId,\n          \"grp\", fooTopicId, \"foo\", 1, 200L, 1, context.time.milliseconds());\n\n      assertTrue(context.hasOffset(\"grp\", \"foo\", 0), \"Regular offset must exist\");\n      assertNotNull(\n          context.offsetMetadataManager.pendingTransactionalOffset(producerId, \"grp\", \"foo\", 1),\n          \"Pending transactional offset must exist before deletion\");\n\n      // Delete topic \"foo\".\n      List<CoordinatorRecord> records =\n          context.deleteTopics(List.of(new DeletedTopic(fooTopicId, \"foo\")));\n\n      // Both the regular and pending transactional offsets must produce tombstones.\n      assertEquals(2, records.size(),\n          \"Both committed and pending transactional offsets must be tombstoned\");\n\n      // Replay the tombstones (simulates the runtime writing + applying them).\n      records.forEach(context::replay);\n\n      // After replay the pending transactional state must also be cleared.\n      assertNull(\n          context.offsetMetadataManager.pendingTransactionalOffset(producerId, \"grp\", \"foo\", 1),\n          \"Pending transactional offset must be cleared after topic deletion tombstone replay\");\n      assertFalse(context.hasOffset(\"grp\", \"foo\", 0),\n          \"Committed offset must be cleared after topic deletion tombstone replay\");\n\n      // Committing the transaction now must NOT resurrect offsets for the deleted topic.\n      context.offsetMetadataManager.replayEndTransactionMarker(producerId, TransactionResult.COMMIT);\n      assertFalse(context.hasOffset(\"grp\", \"foo\", 1),\n          \"Committing the transaction must not restore offsets for a deleted topic\");\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: Exercises the `pendingTransactionalOffsets.forEach` branch in\n  `onTopicsDeleted` (line 1108–1109) which currently has zero test coverage. Also\n  covers the `replayOffsetCommit` tombstone path as it applies to entries in\n  `pendingTransactionalOffsets` via `openTransactions.forEach + pendingOffsets.remove`\n  (lines 1197–1203), and verifies the end-to-end invariant that a topic deletion\n  followed by a transactional commit does not resurrect offsets for the deleted topic.\n\n---\n\n## File References\n\n| File | Role |\n|------|------|\n| `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java` | Core group lifecycle; contains all five code locations above |\n| `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java` | Classic group state machine; `remove()` does not complete `awaitingSyncFuture` |\n| `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java` | Offset commit/expiry; `onTopicsDeleted` covers pending transactional offsets without tests |\n| `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManagerTest.java` | Existing test file; 377 tests across classic and modern group paths |\n| `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManagerTest.java` | Existing offset test file; `testOnTopicsDeleted*` series does not include transactional offsets |\n| `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.java` | Test harness used by all proposed tests |\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
